from pathlib import Path

# Create the directory to save the files
base_path = Path("/mnt/data/tendprocure_github_bootstrap")
base_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# File contents for each requested artifact

# 1. .devcontainer/devcontainer.json
devcontainer_json = """{
  "name": "tendprocure-dev",
  "image": "mcr.microsoft.com/devcontainers/javascript-node:18",
  "features": {
    "ghcr.io/devcontainers/features/github-cli:1": {}
  },
  "postCreateCommand": "npm install",
  "customizations": {
    "vscode": {
      "extensions": [
        "esbenp.prettier-vscode",
        "dbaeumer.vscode-eslint",
        "ms-azuretools.vscode-docker"
      ]
    }
  },
  "mounts": [
    "source=${localWorkspaceFolder}/.env,target=/workspace/.env,type=bind"
  ],
  "remoteUser": "node"
}
"""

# 2. .github/workflows/deploy.yml
github_actions_ci = """name: CI/CD Deploy

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - name: Checkout repo
        uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: 18

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm install

      - name: Build
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        run: vercel --prod --token=${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
"""

# 3. Supabase Edge Function boilerplate (basic hello world)
supabase_edge_function = """import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts'

serve(async (req) => {
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ message: 'Hello from Supabase Edge Functions!' }), {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  })
})
"""

# 4. Frontend route scaffold (Next.js routing structure)
frontend_routes_md = """# TendProcure Frontend Route Plan (Next.js)

## Pages
- `/` - Home
- `/login` - Login
- `/register` - Register
- `/dashboard/admin`
- `/dashboard/vendor`
- `/dashboard/contractor`
- `/dashboard/pm`
- `/dashboard/finance`
- `/tenders` - All active tenders
- `/tender/[id]` - Tender detail
- `/submit-bid/[tenderId]` - Bid submission
- `/contracts/[contractId]` - Contract detail
- `/reports` - Analytics and reporting
- `/notifications` - User alerts
- `/settings` - Profile and settings
"""

# Save the files

(base_path / "deploy.yml").write_text(github_actions_ci)
(base_path / "supabase_hello_world.ts").write_text(supabase_edge_function)
(base_path / "frontend_routes.md").write_text(frontend_routes_md)

from zipfile import ZipFile
import os

# Define base directory for the structure
base_dir = "/mnt/data/tendprocure_project_export"
os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)

# 1. devcontainer.json
devcontainer_content = """
{
  "name": "tendprocure-dev",
  "image": "mcr.microsoft.com/devcontainers/javascript-node:18",
  "features": {
    "ghcr.io/devcontainers/features/github-cli:1": {}
  },
  "postCreateCommand": "npm install",
  "customizations": {
    "vscode": {
      "extensions": [
        "esbenp.prettier-vscode",
        "dbaeumer.vscode-eslint",
        "ms-azuretools.vscode-docker"
      ]
    }
  },
  "mounts": [
    "source=${localWorkspaceFolder}/.env,target=/workspace/.env,type=bind"
  ],
  "remoteUser": "node"
}
"""
os.makedirs(f"{base_dir}/.devcontainer", exist_ok=True)
with open(f"{base_dir}/.devcontainer/devcontainer.json", "w") as f:
    f.write(devcontainer_content.strip())

# 2. GitHub Actions CI/CD workflow
ci_cd_content = """
name: CI/CD Deploy

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: 18

      - run: npm install
      - run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        run: vercel --prod --token=${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
"""
os.makedirs(f"{base_dir}/.github/workflows", exist_ok=True)
with open(f"{base_dir}/.github/workflows/deploy.yml", "w") as f:
    f.write(ci_cd_content.strip())

# 3. Supabase Edge Function
supabase_function = """
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts'

serve(async (req) => {
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ message: 'Hello from Supabase Edge Functions!' }), {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
  })
})
"""
os.makedirs(f"{base_dir}/supabase/functions", exist_ok=True)
with open(f"{base_dir}/supabase/functions/hello_world.ts", "w") as f:
    f.write(supabase_function.strip())

A full-featured tender management and procurement platform powered by Supabase, Vercel, and GitHub Codespaces.

with open(f"{base_dir}/README.md", "w") as f:
    f.write(readme_content.strip())

os.makedirs(f"{base_dir}/assets", exist_ok=True)

with ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(base_dir):
        for file in files:
            file_path = os.path.join(root, file)
            arcname = os.path.relpath(file_path, base_dir)
            zipf.write(file_path, arcname)

## üß† Tech Stack

- Frontend: Next.js + Tailwind CSS

‚úÖ SQL Schema for Supabase
Here‚Äôs your scaffold-ready schema:

sql
Copy
Edit
-- users
CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  role TEXT NOT NULL,
  name TEXT,
  email TEXT UNIQUE,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

-- tenders
CREATE TABLE tenders (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  title TEXT NOT NULL,
  description TEXT,
  status TEXT,
  created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

-- bids
CREATE TABLE bids (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  tender_id UUID REFERENCES tenders(id),
  vendor_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  amount NUMERIC,
  documents TEXT[],
  status TEXT,
  submitted_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT now()
);

-- contracts
CREATE TABLE contracts (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  tender_id UUID REFERENCES tenders(id),
  vendor_id UUID REFERENCES users(id),
  pdf_link TEXT,
  status TEXT,
  start_date DATE,
  end_date DATE,
  signed BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE
);
‚úÖ Supabase Edge Function Templates
generate-pdf.ts
ts
Copy
Edit
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req) => {
  const data = await req.json();
  const contractHTML = `<html><body><h1>${data.title}</h1><p>${data.body}</p></body></html>`;

  // Assume we use an external PDF service
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ pdf_url: "https://fakeurl.com/contract.pdf" }), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }
  });
});

You are the AI onboarding assistant for TendProcure. Your job is to guide new vendors through the full 19-step tender workflow. Start with:

1. Collect company info
2. Prequalification
3. Show available tenders
4. Assist with bid submission
5. Monitor deadlines
6. Auto-scan compliance documents
7. Contract preview & digital signing
8. Start work logs, etc...

Make sure responses are supportive, step-by-step, and personalized to each vendor.

üîê Supabase Edge Function Script: /ai-vendor-help
Here‚Äôs a starter boilerplate for your ai-vendor-help Edge Function (TypeScript):

ts
Copy
Edit
// supabase/functions/ai-vendor-help/index.ts

import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std@0.168.0/http/server.ts"
import { createClient } from "https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js@2.16.0"

serve(async (req) => {
  const { vendor_id, query } = await req.json()

  const supabase = createClient(
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL")!,
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")!
  )

  const { data: vendor } = await supabase
    .from("vendors")
    .select("*")
    .eq("id", vendor_id)
    .single()

  // Placeholder AI logic for response (you can replace this with OpenAI call)
  const ai_response = `Hello ${vendor?.company_name}, based on your query "${query}", here's what you need to do next...`

  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ message: ai_response }), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    status: 200
  })
})
‚úÖ This function should be saved as /supabase/functions/ai-vendor-help/index.ts in your repo.

üó£Ô∏è Voice Command API Hook (Next.js + Web Speech API)
You can integrate this into your chatbot UI frontend:

tsx
Copy
Edit
// components/VoiceCommand.tsx

import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from 'react'

export default function VoiceCommand({ onTranscript }: { onTranscript: (text: string) => void }) {
  const [listening, setListening] = useState(false)
  const recognitionRef = useRef<SpeechRecognition | null>(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || (window as any).webkitSpeechRecognition
    if (!SpeechRecognition) return

    const recognition = new SpeechRecognition()
    recognition.lang = 'en-US'
    recognition.interimResults = false
    recognition.onresult = (e) => onTranscript(e.results[0][0].transcript)
    recognitionRef.current = recognition
  }, [onTranscript])

  const handleListen = () => {
    if (recognitionRef.current) {
      setListening(true)
      recognitionRef.current.start()
    }
  }

  return (
    <button onClick={handleListen} className="btn-voice">
      üéôÔ∏è Speak
    </button>
  )
}
Hook it into your chatbot like:

tsx
Copy
Edit
<VoiceCommand onTranscript={(msg) => sendMessage(msg)} />

from zipfile import ZipFile
import os

# Define the folder where the markdown prompts are located
markdown_folder = "/mnt/data/ai_prompts_markdown_pack"

# Create a zip file containing all the files in the markdown folder
zip_path = "/mnt/data/ai_prompts_markdown_pack_final.zip"
with ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for foldername, subfolders, filenames in os.walk(markdown_folder):
        for filename in filenames:
            file_path = os.path.join(foldername, filename)
            arcname = os.path.relpath(file_path, markdown_folder)
            zipf.write(file_path, arcname=arcname)

‚úÖ Supabase Edge Function: AI Hook Sample
Here‚Äôs the base of your functions/chat-handler.ts:

ts
Copy
Edit
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts'
import { createClient } from 'https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js'

serve(async (req) => {
  const { query } = await req.json()
  const supabase = createClient(Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL"), Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY"))
  
  const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc('semantic_vendor_search', { query })
  if (error) return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error }), { status: 500 })

  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ matches: data }), {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
  })
})

Copy

Let‚Äôs fuel the backend of TendProcure with a powerful Supabase schema and intelligent AI prompt sets‚Äîdesigned to be multilingual, modular, and role-aware. This foundation will supercharge your AI assistant‚Äôs memory, vendor matching, and semantic retrieval.

üß† Supabase SQL Schema Setup
These schemas align with your AI assistant, tender lifecycle, contract tracking, vendor scoring, and multilingual onboarding needs.

üîπ users Table
sql
Copy
Edit
create table users (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  email text unique not null,
  role text check (role in ('admin', 'vendor', 'contractor', 'finance', 'pm')) not null,
  full_name text,
  language_preference text default 'en',
  created_at timestamp default now()
);
üîπ tenders Table
sql
Copy
Edit
create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  title text not null,
  description text,
  status text check (status in ('draft', 'published', 'closed', 'awarded')) default 'draft',
  created_by uuid references users(id),
  start_date date,
  end_date date,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);
üîπ bids Table
sql
Copy
Edit
create table bids (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  vendor_id uuid references users(id),
  bid_amount numeric,
  bid_document_url text,
  status text default 'submitted',
  created_at timestamp default now()
);
üîπ contracts Table
sql
Copy
Edit
create table contracts (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  contractor_id uuid references users(id),
  pdf_url text,
  signed boolean default false,
  start_date date,
  end_date date,
  performance_rating int,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);
üîπ chat_logs Table (AI Assistant Memory)
sql
Copy
Edit
create table chat_logs (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  user_id uuid references users(id),
  message text,
  response text,
  timestamp timestamp default now()
);
üîπ documents Table (For PDF + RAG Indexing)
sql
Copy
Edit
create table documents (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  name text,
  type text,
  content text, -- For semantic embeddings
  embedding vector(1536),
  created_at timestamp default now()
);
üîπ vendor_scores Table
sql
Copy
Edit
create table vendor_scores (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  vendor_id uuid references users(id),
  risk_level int,
  success_rate float,
  fraud_score float,
  last_reviewed timestamp
);

from pathlib import Path

# Define file content for each required file
config_ts = '''\
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'

const supabaseUrl = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!
const supabaseAnonKey = process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY!

export const supabase = createClient(supabaseUrl, supabaseAnonKey)
'''

env_example = '''\
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=https://your-supabase-instance.supabase.co
NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=your-anon-key
OPENAI_API_KEY=your-openai-api-key
SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY=your-service-role-key
SUPABASE_DB_URL=postgresql://user:password@db.supabase.co:5432/postgres
'''

ai_agent_ts = '''\
import { OpenAI } from 'openai'
import { supabase } from '../supabase/config'

const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY })

export async function getChatResponse(userId: string, message: string) {
  const memory = await supabase
    .from('chat_logs')
    .select('message, response')
    .eq('user_id', userId)
    .order('timestamp', { ascending: false })
    .limit(5)

  const context = memory.data?.map(entry => `Q: ${entry.message}\\nA: ${entry.response}`).join('\\n') || ''

  const completion = await openai.chat.completions.create({
    model: 'gpt-4',
    messages: [
      { role: 'system', content: 'You are a helpful assistant for tender and procurement workflows.' },
      { role: 'user', content: context + '\\n' + message }
    ]
  })

  const response = completion.choices[0].message.content

  await supabase.from('chat_logs').insert({
    user_id: userId,
    message,
    response
  })

  return response
}
'''

embedding_script = '''\
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
import { OpenAI } from 'openai'
import fs from 'fs'

const supabase = createClient(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL, process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY)
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY })

async function embedAndStore(docPath, tag) {
  const content = fs.readFileSync(docPath, 'utf-8')
  const embedding = await openai.embeddings.create({
    model: 'text-embedding-ada-002',
    input: content
  })

  const vector = embedding.data[0].embedding

  await supabase.from('documents').insert({
    name: tag,
    type: 'text',
    content,
    embedding: vector
  })

  console.log(`Embedded and stored: ${tag}`)
}

embedAndStore('./docs/tender_guide.md', 'tender_guide')
'''

chat_route_tsx = '''\
import { useState } from 'react'
import { getChatResponse } from '../../ai-assistant/ai-agent'

export default function ChatPage() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)

  const handleSend = async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    const userId = 'user-123' // replace with actual session ID or context
    const response = await getChatResponse(userId, input)
    setMessages([...messages, { role: 'user', text: input }, { role: 'ai', text: response }])
    setInput('')
    setLoading(false)
  }

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: 20 }}>
      <h2>TendProcure Assistant</h2>
      <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
        {messages.map((msg, i) => (
          <p key={i}><strong>{msg.role}:</strong> {msg.text}</p>
        ))}
      </div>
      <input value={input} onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Ask something..." />
      <button onClick={handleSend} disabled={loading}>{loading ? 'Thinking...' : 'Send'}</button>
    </div>
  )
}
'''

ü§ñ ai-assistant/ai-agent.ts
ts
Copy
Edit
import { OpenAI } from 'openai'
import { supabase } from '../supabase/config'

const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY })

export async function getChatResponse(userId: string, message: string) {
  const memory = await supabase
    .from('chat_logs')
    .select('message, response')
    .eq('user_id', userId)
    .order('timestamp', { ascending: false })
    .limit(5)

  const context = memory.data?.map(entry => `Q: ${entry.message}\nA: ${entry.response}`).join('\n') || ''

  const completion = await openai.chat.completions.create({
    model: 'gpt-4',
    messages: [
      { role: 'system', content: 'You are an AI assistant for TendProcure helping with procurement workflows.' },
      { role: 'user', content: context + '\n' + message }
    ]
  })

  const response = completion.choices[0].message.content

  await supabase.from('chat_logs').insert({
    user_id: userId,
    message,
    response
  })

  return response
}
üìú scripts/embed-documents.ts
ts
Copy

import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js'
import { OpenAI } from 'openai'
import fs from 'fs'

const supabase = createClient(process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL!, process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY!)
const openai = new OpenAI({ apiKey: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY! })

async function embedAndStore(docPath: string, tag: string) {
  const content = fs.readFileSync(docPath, 'utf-8')
  const embedding = await openai.embeddings.create({
    model: 'text-embedding-ada-002',
    input: content
  })

  await supabase.from('documents').insert({
    name: tag,
    type: 'text',
    content,
    embedding: embedding.data[0].embedding
  })

  console.log(`‚úÖ Embedded: ${tag}`)
}

embedAndStore('./docs/tender_guide.md', 'Tender Guide')
üß≠ pages/chat/index.tsx (Next.js route)
tsx
Copy
Edit
import { useState } from 'react'
import { getChatResponse } from '../../ai-assistant/ai-agent'

export default function Chat() {
  const [messages, setMessages] = useState<any[]>([])
  const [input, setInput] = useState('')
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false)

  const send = async () => {
    setLoading(true)
    const response = await getChatResponse('user-123', input)
    setMessages([...messages, { role: 'user', text: input }, { role: 'ai', text: response }])
    setInput('')
    setLoading(false)
  }

  return (
    <div className="p-8">
      <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">TendProcure Assistant</h1>
      <div className="my-4 space-y-2">
        {messages.map((m, i) => (
          <p key={i}><strong>{m.role}:</strong> {m.text}</p>
        ))}
      </div>
      <input
        value={input}
        onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="Ask anything..."
        className="border px-3 py-2 rounded mr-2"
      />
      <button onClick={send} disabled={loading}>
        {loading ? 'Thinking...' : 'Send'}
      </button>
    </div>
  )
}

name: Deploy to Vercel

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm install

      - name: Build Vite App
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v25
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_PROJECT_ID }}
          working-directory: ./

from datetime import datetime

‚úÖ GitHub Actions YAML for CI/CD with Vercel + Supabase

Copy
Edit
name: Deploy TendProcure

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
  workflow_dispatch:

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

    steps:
      - name: Checkout repo
        uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: 18

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm install

      - name: Build project
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v25
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_PROJECT_ID }}
          working-directory: ./
Make sure to add the Vercel secrets in your GitHub repo settings.

name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main ]
  pull_request:

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Setup Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: 18

      - name: Install Dependencies
        run: npm install

      - name: Build App
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v25
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_PROJECT_ID }}
          working-directory: ./

      - name: Sync Supabase Schema
        run: supabase db push
        env:
          SUPABASE_ACCESS_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SUPABASE_TOKEN }}

### ‚úÖ Supabase Edge Function Boilerplate

**`supabase/functions/vendor-match.ts`**

```ts
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts';
import { createClient } from 'https://esm.sh/@supabase/supabase-js';

serve(async (req) => {
  const supabase = createClient(
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL"),
    Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")
  );

  const { query } = await req.json();
  const result = await supabase.rpc('semantic_match_vendors', { query });

  return new Response(JSON.stringify(result.data), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
  });
});

‚úÖ Enhanced Vector Logic (Semantic Search)
ts
Copy
Edit
// vectorSearch.ts
import { createClient } from '@supabase/supabase-js';
import { similaritySearch } from './embedding';

const supabase = createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_KEY);

export async function findBestVendors(query: string) {
  const embedding = await similaritySearch(query);
  const { data } = await supabase.rpc('match_vendors_by_embedding', {
    query_embedding: embedding,
    match_threshold: 0.78,
    match_count: 10
  });
  return data;
}
Supabase Function (SQL):

sql
Copy
Edit
create or replace function match_vendors_by_embedding(
  query_embedding vector,
  match_threshold float,
  match_count int
)
returns table(id uuid, name text, similarity float) as $$
  select
    v.id,
    v.name,
    1 - (v.embedding <=> query_embedding) as similarity
  from vendor_profiles v
  where 1 - (v.embedding <=> query_embedding) > match_threshold
  order by similarity desc
  limit match_count;
$$ language sql;

‚úÖ Finalized Supabase SQL Schema
sql
Copy
Edit
-- vendors
create table vendors (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  name text,
  email text unique,
  location text,
  service_categories text[],
  embedding vector(1536)
);

-- tenders
create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  title text,
  description text,
  deadline timestamp,
  created_by uuid references users(id),
  embedding vector(1536)
);

-- bids
create table bids (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  vendor_id uuid references vendors(id),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  amount numeric,
  status text,
  submitted_at timestamp default now()
);

‚úÖ 7. SQL Table Scaffold (for Supabase)
sql
Copy
Edit
-- Escrow Table
create table escrow (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  vendor_id uuid references users(id),
  amount numeric,
  status text default 'PENDING',
  milestones jsonb,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

-- Disputes
create table disputes (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  opened_by uuid references users(id),
  status text,
  summary text,
  chat_history jsonb,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

# TendProcure ‚Äì AI-Enhanced Tender Management

TendProcure is a secure, multilingual, AI-powered tender and vendor management platform built using **Vite + React**, **Supabase**, and **Deno Edge Functions**.

## üß† Features

- AI Assistant with memory, RAG, & export
- Vendor Recommendation Engine (vector search)
- Escrow Logic + Smart Contracts
- Dispute AI & Fraud Scoring
- Infographics & PDF Generators
- Modular React codebase with full CI/CD

## üöÄ Setup

```bash
git clone https://github.com/mcruz-lez/tender-flow-pro
cd tender-flow-pro
npm install
npm run dev

          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.PROJECT_ID }}
          working-directory: .

üß¨ Supabase SQL Schema Scaffold (pgvector included)
Located in src/supabase/migrations/schema.sql

sql
Copy
Edit
create extension if not exists vector;

create table vendors (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  name text,
  service_area text,
  languages text[],
  embedding vector(1536),
  rating float
);

create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  title text,
  description text,
  requirements jsonb,
  deadline timestamp
);

create table chats (
  id serial primary key,
  session_id uuid,
  user_role text,
  message text,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

# Define project directory structure

folders = [
    ".devcontainer",
    ".github/workflows",
    "public/assets/templates",
    "src/ai/assistantPrompts/multilingual",
    "src/ai/rag",

    "src/styles"
]

with ZipFile(zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(base_path):
        for file in files:
            abs_path = os.path.join(root, file)
            rel_path = os.path.relpath(abs_path, base_path)

üìÑ README.md (Starter Template)

Copy

# üèóÔ∏è TendProcure ‚Äì Tender Management Platform

TendProcure is a full-stack, AI-powered tender and procurement platform built with **Vite + React**, **Supabase**, and **Lovable.dev** support.

## üì¶ Stack
- Frontend: Vite + React
- Backend: Supabase (PostgreSQL, Edge Functions, pgvector)
- CI/CD: GitHub Actions + Vercel
- AI: GPT-4o Agent, RAG, multilingual onboarding, analytics
- Hosting: Vercel, GitHub Codespaces

## üß† AI Features
- Role-based AI Assistant with multilingual onboarding
- PDF generation (contracts, reports)
- Vendor recommendation via embeddings
- Dispute resolution and fraud scoring engine
- Escrow logic for payment workflows

## üìä Dashboards
- Dynamic Chart.js analytics
- Admin panel for usage logs
- Vendor KPIs and performance summaries

## üîß Scripts
```bash
npm run dev        # Start Vite dev server
npm run build      # Production build
npm run supabase   # Launch Supabase CLI
üõ†Ô∏è Project Setup
Clone this repo

Run npm install

Connect Supabase project via CLI

Deploy with Vercel or GitHub Pages

yaml
Copy
Edit

---

### ‚öôÔ∏è `.github/workflows/deploy.yml` (Vercel CI/CD)

```yaml
name: Deploy to Vercel

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - name: Install Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '20'
      - run: npm install
      - run: npm run build
      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        run: npx vercel --prod --token=${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
üî• Supabase Edge Function Scaffold
/supabase/functions/sendNotification/index.ts

ts
Copy
Edit
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts'

serve(async (req) => {
  const { userId, message } = await req.json()
  // Push logic here: Insert into Supabase table or call webhook
  return new Response(JSON.stringify({ status: 'Notification sent' }), {
    headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" }
  })
})

create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  title text,
  status text,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

create table bids (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  vendor_id uuid,
  amount numeric,
  status text,
  submitted_at timestamp default now()
);

create table notifications (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id uuid,
  message text,
  read boolean default false,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

name: Deploy Vite React App

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

      - name: Set up Node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: 18

      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: Build app
        run: npm run build

      - name: Deploy to Vercel
        uses: amondnet/vercel-action@v20
        with:
          vercel-token: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
          vercel-org-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_ORG_ID }}
          vercel-project-id: ${{ secrets.VERCEL_PROJECT_ID }}
          working-directory: ./

üß† Supabase SQL Scaffold (Minimal, pgvector enabled)
sql
Copy
Edit
-- Enable vector extension
create extension if not exists vector;

-- Vendors
create table vendors (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  name text,
  service_type text,
  documents jsonb,
  prequalified boolean default false,
  embeddings vector(1536)
);

-- Tenders
create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  title text,
  description text,
  requirements jsonb,
  deadline timestamp,
  status text
);

-- Bids
create table bids (
  id uuid primary key default uuid_generate_v4(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  vendor_id uuid references vendors(id),
  documents jsonb,
  status text,
  score float
);

### 4. **Sample Supabase Edge Function**

File: `supabase/edge-functions/vendor-match.ts`

```ts
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req) => {
  const input = await req.json();
  const { query } = input;

  const embedding = await fetch("https://api.openai.com/v1/embeddings", {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${Deno.env.get("OPENAI_KEY")}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      input: query,
      model: "text-embedding-ada-002"
    })
  }).then(res => res.json());

  return new Response(JSON.stringify(embedding.data), { status: 200 });
});

with ZipFile(zip_path, "w") as zipf:
    for root, _, files in os.walk(base_dir):

            file_path = os.path.join(root, file)
            zipf.write(file_path, os.path.relpath(file_path, base_dir))

# üõ†Ô∏è TendProcure ‚Äì Intelligent Tender Management Platform

This is a smart, multilingual tender management system built using Vite + React, Supabase, and OpenAI-powered AI assistants.

## Features
- üìä Dynamic Analytics Dashboard
- üß† AI Assistant (RAG + Semantic Vendor Matcher)
- üóÉÔ∏è Auto-generated PDF Contracts
- üîÅ Role-based Bid Submission & Evaluation
- üì¶ Supabase pgvector + Edge Functions

## Setup
```bash
git clone https://github.com/mcruz-lez/tender-flow-pro
cd tender-flow-pro
npm install
npm run dev
Documentation

üìÑ Infographics: /public/infographics/

‚úÖ GitHub Actions Workflow (.github/workflows/deploy.yml)
yaml
Copy
Edit
name: Deploy to Vercel

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main]

jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: 20
      - run: npm install
      - run: npm run build
      - run: npx vercel --prod --token=${{ secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN }}
‚úÖ Supabase Edge Function Starter (supabase/edge-functions/vendor-match.ts)
ts
Copy
Edit
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req) => {
  const { query } = await req.json();
  const embedding = await fetch("https://api.openai.com/v1/embeddings", {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${Deno.env.get("OPENAI_KEY")}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({ input: query, model: "text-embedding-ada-002" })
  }).then(res => res.json());

  return new Response(JSON.stringify(embedding.data), { status: 200 });
});

# üìò TendProcure Onboarding Guide

## Steps to Submit a Bid
1. Login or Register
2. Complete your vendor profile
3. Go to `Tenders > New`
4. Fill the tender wizard (docs, price, timeline)
5. Confirm & Submit

## Support
- Email: support@tendprocure.ai
- Chat: Built-in AI Assistant (bottom right)

from zipfile import ZipFile
import os

# Define the directory where all generated assets are stored or will be created.
base_dir = "/mnt/data/TendProcure_Complete_Archive"

# Make sure the base directory exists
os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)

# Subdirectories to simulate organizing assets from beginning to end
folders = [
    "01_Onboarding_Tutorials",
    "02_AI_Assistant_Module",
    "03_Dashboard_Analytics",
    "04_Vendor_Recommendation",
    "05_Notifications_System",
    "06_Contract_PDF_Generator",
    "07_SQL_Schema_and_DB",
    "08_Supabase_Edge_Functions",
    "09_Markdown_Help_Guides",
    "10_Multilingual_Flows",
    "11_Infographics_Visuals",
    "12_Deployment_Configs",
    "13_GitHub_CI_CD",
    "14_Backups_and_CRON",
    "15_Admin_Panel_and_Logs"
]

# Create folder structure inside base_dir
for folder in folders:
    os.makedirs(os.path.join(base_dir, folder), exist_ok=True)

# Define output zip path
output_zip_path = f"{base_dir}.zip"

# Create a zip archive of the entire TendProcure development package
with ZipFile(output_zip_path, 'w') as zipf:
    for root, _, files in os.walk(base_dir):
        for file in files:
            full_path = os.path.join(root, file)
            arcname = os.path.relpath(full_path, start=base_dir)
            zipf.write(full_path, arcname=arcname)

output_zip_path
Result
'/mnt/data/TendProcure_Complete_Archive.zip'

  push: { branches: [main] }

    runs-on: ubuntu-latest

      - uses: actions/checkout@v3

3. supabase/schema.sql
sql
Copy
Edit
create extension if not exists vector;

create table vendors (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  name text not null,
  expertise text[],
  embedding vector(1536),
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  title text,
  description text,
  requirements jsonb,
  deadline timestamp,
  status text
);

create table bids (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  vendor_id uuid references vendors(id),
  documents jsonb,
  amount numeric,
  status text,
  submitted_at timestamp default now()
);

create table notifications (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id uuid,
  message text,
  is_read boolean default false,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);
4. supabase/edge-functions/vendor-match.ts
ts
Copy
Edit
import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req) => {
  const { query } = await req.json();
  const resp = await fetch("https://api.openai.com/v1/embeddings", {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${Deno.env.get("OPENAI_KEY")}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({ input: query, model: "text-embedding-ada-002" })
  });
  const data = await resp.json();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data.data), { status: 200 });
});
5. src/ai/assistant/ai-agent.ts
ts
Copy
Edit
export async function handleMessage(input: string) {
  if (/help/i.test(input)) return "I can guide you through tenders, bids, contracts, onboarding...";
  if (/contract/i.test(input)) return "To generate a contract PDF, use `/generate-contract {tenderId}`.";
  return "I'm here to help with any tender lifecycle question!";
}
6. docs/help-onboarding.md
markdown
Copy
Edit
# ‚úÖ Tender & Vendor Onboarding Guide

## Step 1: Register & Verify Email
## Step 2: Complete your Vendor Profile (documents, services, insurance)
## Step 3: Prequalification walkthrough (you'll need attachments and evidence)
## Step 4: How to browse & apply for Tenders
## Step 5: Bid Submission flow (documents, EMD, markup, final submit)
## Step 6: Contract signing & mobilization instructions
## Step 7: Monitoring (milestones, reporting, payments)

---

Need help? Use the AI chat icon or email support@tendprocure.ai.
üìö Expanded Blog Post Library
Here's a starter batch of robust blog post topics and content to power your CMS:

1. Top 7 Tender Bidding Tips Every Vendor Should Know
markdown
Copy
Edit
---
title: "Top 7 Tender Bidding Tips Every Vendor Should Know"
date: "2025-06-29"
tags: ["bidding", "tender", "vendors", "strategy"]
---

1. Read the NIT carefully.
2. Align with PQ requirements.
3. Do a detailed cost breakdown.
4. Double-check EMD and compliance attachments.
5. Use our AI assistant to catch errors.
6. Review before submission.
7. Monitor for LOA.

output_dir = "/mnt/data/tendprocure_bundle"

# Define content for key files
file_contents = {
    "devcontainer/devcontainer.json": """{
  "name": "TendProcure DevContainer",
  "image": "mcr.microsoft.com/devcontainers/javascript-node:20",
  "postCreateCommand": "npm install",
  "forwardPorts": [5173],
  "customizations": {"vscode":{"extensions":["esbenp.prettier-vscode","dbaeumer.vscode-eslint"]}},
  "settings":{"terminal.integrated.defaultProfile.linux":"bash"}
}""",
    ".github/workflows/deploy.yml": """name: Deploy to Vercel
on:
  push: { branches: [main] }
jobs:
  deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with: { node-version: 20 }
      - run: npm install
      - run: npm run build
      - run: npx vercel --prod --token=${{secrets.VERCEL_TOKEN}}""",
    "supabase/schema.sql": """create extension if not exists vector;

create table vendors (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  name text not null,
  expertise text[],
  embedding vector(1536),
  created_at timestamp default now()
);

create table tenders (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  title text,
  description text,
  requirements jsonb,
  deadline timestamp,
  status text
);

create table bids (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  tender_id uuid references tenders(id),
  vendor_id uuid references vendors(id),
  documents jsonb,
  amount numeric,
  status text,
  submitted_at timestamp default now()
);

create table notifications (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id uuid,
  message text,
  is_read boolean default false,
  created_at timestamp default now()
);""",
    "supabase/edge-functions/vendor-match.ts": """import { serve } from "https://deno.land/std/http/server.ts";

serve(async (req) => {
  const { query } = await req.json();
  const resp = await fetch("https://api.openai.com/v1/embeddings", {
    method: "POST",
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${Deno.env.get("OPENAI_KEY")}`,
      "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({ input: query, model: "text-embedding-ada-002" })
  });
  const data = await resp.json();
  return new Response(JSON.stringify(data.data), { status: 200 });
});""",
    "src/ai/assistant/ai-agent.ts": """export async function handleMessage(input: string) {
  if (/help/i.test(input)) return "I can guide you through tenders, bids, contracts, onboarding...";
  if (/contract/i.test(input)) return "To generate a contract PDF, use `/generate-contract {tenderId}`.";
  return "I'm here to help with any tender lifecycle question!";
}""",
    "docs/help-onboarding.md": """# ‚úÖ Tender & Vendor Onboarding Guide

# Write files to directory
for path, content in file_contents.items():
    full_path = os.path.join(output_dir, path)
    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(full_path), exist_ok=True)
    with open(full_path, "w") as f:
        f.write(content)

# Create zip archive
zip_path = "/mnt/data/TendProcure_DevBundle.zip"
with zipfile.ZipFile(zip_path, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as zipf:
    for foldername, _, filenames in os.walk(output_dir):
        for filename in filenames:
            file_path = os.path.join(foldername, filename)
            arcname = os.path.relpath(file_path, output_dir)
            zipf.write(file_path, arcname)
